<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">1971–72 UEFA Cup</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>

<p><b>1971–72 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_Cup" title="UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a></b> was the inaugural year of the competition, which effectively replaced the <a href="/wiki/Inter-Cities_Fairs_Cup" title="Inter-Cities Fairs Cup">Inter-Cities Fairs Cup</a>.</p>
<p>It was won by English side <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> over their countrymen <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C.">Wolverhampton Wanderers</a> 3–2 on aggregate after a two-legged final.</p>
<p>The tournament was open to the highest-placed European teams that had not qualified for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">European Cup</a> or <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Cup_Winners%27_Cup" title="UEFA Cup Winners' Cup">UEFA Cup Winners' Cup</a>. It commenced on 14 September 1971 and concluded on 17 May 1972. A total of 64 football clubs entered the first round draw.</p>
<p>The tournament's top scorer was <a href="/wiki/Ludwig_Br%C3%BCndl" title="Ludwig Bründl">Ludwig Bründl</a> of Eintracht Braunschweig with 10 goals.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="First_round">First round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971%E2%80%9372_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: First round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The matches were played on 14–16 and 29–30 September 1971. Teams from the same nation could not be drawn against one another.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_round">Second round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971%E2%80%9372_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Second round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The matches were played on 19–21 October and 2–4 November 1971. Teams from the same nation could not be drawn against one another.</p>

<p><i>Juventus won 3–1 on aggregate.</i></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_round">Third round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971%E2%80%9372_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Third round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The matches were played on 23–24 November and 8 December 1971. Teams from the same nation could not be drawn against one another.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_leg_6">Second leg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971%E2%80%9372_UEFA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Second leg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
